Se2- is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to six equivalent K1+ and two equivalent Pt2+ atoms.
K2PtS2 crystallizes in the orthorhombic Immm space group. K1+ is bonded in a 6-coordinate geometry to six equivalent S2- atoms. There are four shorter (3.26 Å) and two longer (3.27 Å) K-S bond lengths. Pt2+ is bonded in a square co-planar geometry to four equivalent S2- atoms. All Pt-S bond lengths are 2.37 Å. S2- is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to six equivalent K1+ and two equivalent Pt2+ atoms.

There are two shorter (3.10 Å) and four longer (3.12 Å) Ca-Pd bond lengths. Mg is bonded in a 4-coordinate geometry to four equivalent Pd atoms. All Mg-Pd bond lengths are 2.67 Å. Pd is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to six equivalent Ca and two equivalent Mg atoms.

PbPdO2 crystallizes in the orthorhombic Imma space group. Pd2+ is bonded in a square co-planar geometry to four equivalent O2- atoms. All Pd-O bond lengths are 2.04 Å. Pb2+ is bonded in a 4-coordinate geometry to four equivalent O2- atoms. All Pb-O bond lengths are 2.36 Å. O2- is bonded to two equivalent Pd2+ and two equivalent Pb2+ atoms to form a mixture of distorted corner and edge-sharing OPd2Pb2 tetrahedra.
La(OsB)4 crystallizes in the tetragonal P42/n space group. La2+ is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent Os2- atoms. All La-Os bond lengths are 3.24 Å. Os2- is bonded in a 4-coordinate geometry to two equivalent La2+ and four equivalent B+1.50+ atoms. There are a spread of Os-B bond distances ranging from 2.15-2.18 Å. B+1.50+ is bonded in a 4-coordinate geometry to four equivalent Os2- atoms.
BaMoO4 crystallizes in the tetragonal I41/a space group. Ba2+ is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent O2- atoms. There are four shorter (2.76 Å) and four longer (2.80 Å) Ba-O bond lengths. Mo6+ is bonded in a tetrahedral geometry to four equivalent O2- atoms. All Mo-O bond lengths are 1.77 Å. O2- is bonded in a distorted single-bond geometry to two equivalent Ba2+ and one Mo6+ atom.
NaAlH4 is Zircon-like structured and crystallizes in the tetragonal I41/a space group. Na1+ is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent H1- atoms. All Na-H bond lengths are 2.37 Å. Al3+ is bonded in a tetrahedral geometry to four equivalent H1- atoms. All Al-H bond lengths are 1.63 Å. H1- is bonded in a distorted trigonal planar geometry to two equivalent Na1+ and one Al3+ atom.
Li4NH crystallizes in the tetragonal I41/a space group. Li1+ is bonded in a trigonal planar geometry to two equivalent N3- and one H1- atom. There is one shorter (2.01 Å) and one longer (2.06 Å) Li-N bond length. The Li-H bond length is 1.90 Å. N3- is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent Li1+ atoms. H1- is bonded in a tetrahedral geometry to four equivalent Li1+ atoms.
TcAgO4 crystallizes in the tetragonal I41/a space group. Tc7+ is bonded in a tetrahedral geometry to four equivalent O2- atoms. All Tc-O bond lengths are 1.72 Å. Ag1+ is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent O2- atoms. There are four shorter (2.48 Å) and four longer (2.58 Å) Ag-O bond lengths. O2- is bonded in a distorted single-bond geometry to one Tc7+ and two equivalent Ag1+ atoms.

BaAu2O4 crystallizes in the tetragonal I41/a space group. Ba2+ is bonded in a 8-coordinate geometry to eight equivalent O2- atoms. All Ba-O bond lengths are 2.78 Å. Au3+ is bonded in a square co-planar geometry to four equivalent O2- atoms. All Au-O bond lengths are 2.01 Å. O2- is bonded to two equivalent Ba2+ and two equivalent Au3+ atoms to form a mixture of distorted corner and edge-sharing OBa2Au2 tetrahedra.

O2- is bonded in a distorted single-bond geometry to one Re7+ and two equivalent Ag1+ atoms.
